***ben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> (29)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a></i>, as an imperative, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered non-standard, the standard form being <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***bende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a> (1923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bend</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bandiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰendʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tie; bond, <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bendes.html>bendes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:benden.html>benden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bendetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a>, squad</li>
<li>mess as in: a disagreeable mixture of a large quantity of <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> in disorder resulting from people misbehaving or animals stampeding.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">beestenbende</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bendeoorlog.html>bendeoorlog</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gideonsbende</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, by analogy of other <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-de</i> verb contractions. The personal agreement <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ungrammatical in standard Dutch, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> based on contamination with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bende.html>bende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.
</p>

***bender.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a> (16573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bend</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. In sense of “heavy drinking”, originally generally “spree”, from 1846,<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-oetyld-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> of uncertain origin – vague contemporary sense of “something extraordinary”, connection to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bend</i> (e.g., bending elbow to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>) or perhaps from Scottish sense of “strong drinker”.<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-oetyld-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">benders</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who, or that which, bends.</li>
<li>A device to aid bending of pipes to a specific angle.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bout of heavy drinking.
<dl><dd><i>He's <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> out on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></b> with his mates.</i></dd></dl>

<dl><dd>A couple of students of Williams College <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to North Adams on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a>.</b> This would have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> serious matter under the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> of circumstances, but each returned with a “brick in his hat,” etc.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A homosexual <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.
<ul><li><b>2004</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alan_Hollinghurst" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alan Hollinghurst">Alan Hollinghurst</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Line_of_Beauty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Line of Beauty">The Line of Beauty</a></i>, Bloomsbury, 2005, Chapter 6,
<dl><dd>“So they're easy about having a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></b> in the house, are they, their lordships?”</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A simple shelter, made using flexible <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a> or withies</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A suspended sentence.
<ul><li><b>2015</b>, Olly Jarvis, <i>Death by Dangerous</i> (page 81)
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:gary.html>Gary</a>, what happened in Ahmed?' 'Not guilty, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>.' <li><b>2019</b>, Howard Williamson, <i>Youth and Policy: Contexts and Consequences</i>
<dl><dd>He anticipated a prison sentence though he thought there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a slight possibility of 'getting off on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a>'</b> (suspended sentence).</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:sixpence.html>sixpence</a>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something exceptional.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In sense “bout of heavy drinking”, usually in form “on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></b>”.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to express disbelief or doubt at what one <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a>.</span> <span class="defdate">[early 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate that the previous phrase <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> meant sarcastically or ironically.</span> <span class="defdate">[early 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a> yes, I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> do it — <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bender.html>bender</a>!</b></i></i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">disbelief</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="see-cites"><i>See</i> Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:bullshit.html>bullshit</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sarcasm</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> think</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">not</span></li></ul>

<p>Created in analogy to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">am</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Modern Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> replaced the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> verb forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bes.html>bes</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(you) are (sg.)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:benul.html>benul</a> (11517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bepalen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a> (2771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put <a href = vnd.unilang:poles.html>poles</a> on/around</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paal.html>paal</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to determine, to figure out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bepaald.html>bepaald</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>determined</b> by law.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to determine, to decide, to choose</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to limit oneself, to restrain  oneself, to contain oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toekomst.html>toekomst</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:proberen.html>proberen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> per <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mezelf.html>mezelf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the future, I will try to <b>limit myself</b> to only two per day.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bepalinge</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beperking.html>beperking</a> (25893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beperken.html>beperken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beperking.html>beperking</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beperkingen.html>beperkingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beperking.html>beperkinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***beraden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beraden.html>beraden</a> (45833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">berâden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">birādan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raden.html>raden</a></i>.
